   Suvarṇaprabhāsasūtram	SuvarNa-praBAsa-sUtram
   // suvarṇaprabhāsottamasūtrendrarājaḥ //	// suvarNa-praBAsa-uttama-sUtrendra-rAjaH //
   // nidānaparivartaḥ //	// nidAna-parivartaH //
   om namaḥ śrīsarvabuddhabodhisattvebhyaḥ /	om namaH SrI-sarva-budDa-boDisattveByaH /
   om namaḥ śrībhagavatyai āryaprajñāpāramitāyai // tadyathā /	om namaH SrI-BagavatyE Arya-prajQApAramitAyE // tat-yaTA /
   om śrutismṛtigativijaye svāhā //	om Sruti-smRti-gati-vijaye svAhA //
   yasmin pāramitā daśottamaguṇāstaistairnayaiḥ sūcitāḥ	yasmin pAramitAH daSa-uttama-guNAH-tEH-tEH-nayEH sUcitAH
   sarvajñena jagaddhitāya daśa ca prakhyāpitā bhūmayaḥ /	sarvajQena jagat-hitAya daSa ca praKyApitA BUmayaH /
   ucchedadhruvavarjitā ca vimalā proktā gatirmadhyamā	ucCeda-Druva-varjitA ca vimalA proktA gatiH-maDyamA

   śrutaṃ mayaikasamaye gṛdhrakūṭe tathāgataḥ //	Srutam mayA-eka-samaye gRDrakUwe taTAgataH //

   bodhisattvasamuccayayā mahākuladevatayā, sarasvatyā ca mahādevatayā, śriyā	boDisattva-samuccayayA mahA-kula-devatayA, sarasvatyA ca mahAdevatayA, SriyA
   ca mahādevatayā, dṛḍhayā ca mahāpṛthivīdevatayā, hārītyā ca mahādevatayā,	ca mahAdevatayA, dRXayA ca mahA-pRTivI-devatayA, hArItyA ca mahAdeva-tayA,
   evaṃ	evam
   pramukhābhirmahādevatābhiranekadevanāgayakṣarākṣasagandharvāsuragaruḍakinnaramahoragamanuṣyāmanuṣyaiḥ	pramuKABiH-mahAdevatABiH-aneka-deva-nAga-yakza-rAkzasa-ganDarva-asura-garuxa-kinnara-mahA-uraga-manuzya-amanuzyEH

   bhagavandharmavinayaṃ bhaviṣyatīti?	Bagavan-Darma-vinayam Bavizyati-iti?

   dharmasāraṃ pratiṣṭhitam /	DarmasAram pratizWitam /

   (Bagchi 2)	(Baj-Ci 2)

   śṛṇvanti ya idaṃ sūtraṃ gambhīraṃ buddhagocaram /	SRNvanti yaH idam sUtram gamBIram budDa-gocaram /

   (Bagchi 3)	(Baj-Ci 3)

   uptakuśalamūlāste bahubuddhaprakāśitāḥ /	upta-kuSala-mUlAH-te bahu-budDa-prakASitAH /

   iti śrīsuvarṇaprabhāsottamasūtrendrarāje nidānaparivartto nāma prathamaḥ	iti SrI-suvarNa-praBAsa-uttama-sUtrendra-rAje nidAnaparivarttaH nAma praTamaH
   (Bagchi 4)	(Baj-Ci 4)
   // Tathāgatāyuḥpramāṇanirdeśaparivartaḥ //	// TaTA-gata-AyuH-pramANa-nirdeSa-parivartaH //

   dīrghāyuṣkatāyām / katamau dvau prāṇātipātaviramaṇaṃ bhojanapradānaṃ ca /	dIrGa-Ayuzka-tAyAm / katamO dvO prANa-atipAta-viramaNam Bojana-pradAnam ca /

   vaiḍūryamayamanekadivyaratnapratyuptaṃ tathāgatavigrahaṃ divyātikrāntena	vExUrya-mayam-aneka-divya-ratna-pratyuptam taTAgata-vigraham divya-atikrAntena

   paryaṅkāni divyaratnapuṣpapatraiḥ prajñaptāni prādurbhūtāni babhūvaḥ /	paryaFkAni divya-ratna-puzpa-patrEH prajQaptAni prAdurBUtAni baBUvaH /

   prādurbhūtāni / teṣu ca padmeṣu catvāro buddhā bhagavantaḥ prādurbhūtāḥ	prAdurBUtAni / tezu ca padmezu catvAraH budDAH BagavantaH prAdurBUtAH
   babhuvuḥ / purāntikena tvakṣobhyastathāgataḥ prādurbhūto dakṣiṇena	baBuvuH / pura-antikena tu-akzoByaH-taTAgataH prAdurBUtaH dakziNena
   ratnaketustathāgataḥ prādurbhūtaḥ paścimenāmitāyustathāgataḥ prādurbhūta	ratnaketuH-taTAgataH prAdurBUtaH paScimena-amita-AyuH-taTAgataH prAdurBUta

   / kathametat,kimetad yadbhagavataḥ śākyamunerevaṃ parīttamāyuḥpramāṇaṃ	/ kaTam-etat-,kim-etat yat-BagavataH SAkya-muneH-evam parIttam-AyuH-pramANam
   yadutāśīti varṣāṇi /	yat-uta-aSIti varzANi /

   bodhisattvametadavocan / mā tvaṃ kulaputraivaṃ cintaya evaṃ parīttaṃ	boDisattvam-etat-avocan / mA tvam kula-putra-evam cintayaH evam parIttam
   bhagavataḥ śākyamunerāyuḥpramāṇam / tatkasya hetoḥ / na ca vai kulaputra	BagavataH SAkya-muneH-AyuH-pramANam / tat-kasya hetoH / na ca vE kula-putra
